# Fork vs Upstream ‚Äî Feature Matrix

**Status.** **Live.** Updated whenever a feature ships, a design doc
lands, or upstream cuts a new release.
**Snapshot date.** 2026-05-19.
**Upstream baseline.** `gitlab.com/dlr-shepard/shepard 5.2.0`.

This is the **progress tracker** comparing what's available in this
fork (`noheton/shepard main`) against the upstream 5.2.0 surface,
broken down by feature area. **Different from `aidocs/34`** ‚Äî that
doc is admin-facing ("what an upgrader needs to know about each
landed change"); this doc is **contributor / PI-facing** ("how does
this fork compare across the whole feature surface, including
designed-not-yet-shipped work").

## Status legend

| Symbol | Meaning |
|---|---|
| **‚úì** | **Feature-complete** ‚Äî backend logic shipped AND UI accepted on `main` |
| **‚öô** | **Dev-track** ‚Äî backend shipped; UI missing or not yet accepted. Not feature-complete. |
| **üÖ∞Ô∏è** | **Alpha (UI placeholder)** ‚Äî backend shipped; UI surface is a placeholder stub from `frontend/components/common/placeholder/` (per CLAUDE.md "a feature with a placeholder UI is `alpha`, not `beta` and not `shipped`", codified 2026-05-30). Distinct from **‚öô** because there IS a UI present ‚Äî it's a stub mount, not a missing surface; the work is to replace the stub with a real implementation. Tracked under `PLACEHOLDER-REPLACE-<ID>` in `aidocs/16`. |
| **üìê** | Designed (design doc landed; implementation queued) |
| **üöß** | Implementation in flight (agent dispatched / PR open) |
| **=** | Parity with upstream (same shape on both sides) |
| **‚Üë** | This fork extends upstream (we ship more) |
| **‚Äî** | Not implemented anywhere |
| **‚öÝ** | Diverges deliberately ‚Äî see notes |

**Feature-complete definition:** A feature reaches **‚úì** only when both (a) the backend logic
is on `main` and (b) the UI surface is accepted ‚Äî the full user-facing flow works end to end.
Backend-only rows stay at **‚öô** until the UI ships and is verified. This prevents the matrix
from over-counting progress.

## Dev track

Features with complete backend logic but no accepted UI. These are **not** feature-complete
and should be prioritised for UI work before being promoted to **‚úì**.

| Feature | Backend slice | UI gap | Refs |
|---|---|---|---|
| **AI1c** Channel quality scoring | `qualityScore ‚àà [0,1]` field computed + stored on `TimeseriesReference` | Score never displayed in the TS reference panel or chart header | `aidocs/43 ¬ß3.2` |
| **TM1a** Time-reference model | `PATCH /v2/timeseries-references/{appId}` ‚Äî `timeReference` + `wallClockOffset` + `wallClockOffsetSource` fields | No edit UI in the TS reference detail page; fields invisible to users | `aidocs/16 TM1a` |
| **N1f** SPARQL proxy | `GET/POST /v2/semantic/{repoAppId}/sparql` ‚Äî read-only SELECT/ASK against n10s; 37+21 unit tests | No query interface anywhere in the frontend | `aidocs/16 N1f` |
| **A5a/A5b/A5c/A5d** HDF5 containers + per-DataObject references | HdfContainer CRUD + permission bridge + offline download + HdfReference per-DataObject anchor (`/v2/data-objects/{appId}/hdf-references` GET/POST/DELETE) | No HDF container UI (list, create, browse datasets, download); HdfReferencesPane wired to DataObject detail | `aidocs/35` + `aidocs/63 ADR-0020` |
| **A5c-annotation** HDF5 annotation affordance | `hdf` vocabulary (V87) + `hdf-shapes.ttl` SHACL shape + Annotate button in HdfReferencesPane | ‚Äî | `aidocs/16` A5c-annotation |
| ~~**PV1a/PV1b** Payload version history~~ | ~~`GET /v2/{file,structured-data}-containers/{id}/files/{name}/versions` ‚Äî per-upload SHA-256 + version counter~~ | **Promoted to ‚úì** ‚Äî `PayloadVersionHistoryDialog.vue` + `useFetchPayloadVersions` + 8 Vitest tests shipped; history icon on every file row; >100 MB confirm guard | `aidocs/46` |
| **FS1e1/FS1e2** File storage migration | `POST /v2/admin/files/migrate` + status endpoint + auto-sweep scheduler | No migration trigger or progress UI in AdminStoragePane; CLI only | `aidocs/45 ¬ß6` |
| ~~**F3** Permission audit log~~ | ~~`GET /v2/admin/permission-audit/log` ‚Äî GRANT/UPDATE/REVOKE events with actor/entityAppId/from/to filters~~ | **Promoted to ‚úì** ‚Äî `PermissionAuditLogPane.vue` + `useFetchPermissionAuditLog` + `AdminPermissionAuditApi` shipped; filters for entityAppId/actor/from/to; paginated table with action chips | `aidocs/16 F3` |
| ~~**#68** Admin activity log viewer~~ | ~~`GET /v2/provenance/activities` ‚Äî instance-wide provenance stream; admins see all rows unfiltered~~ | **Promoted to ‚úì** ‚Äî `AdminActivityLogPane.vue` + `useFetchAdminActivities` composable shipped; server-side agent/targetKind/targetAppId filters; client-side text + action-kind chip filters; load-more pagination (100 batch); density-compact `v-table` with action-kind chips + status colour coding; `AdminFragments.ACTIVITY_LOG` + menu entry + landing card wired in `admin/index.vue` | `aidocs/16 #68` |
| **J1d** Lab journal edit history | `GET /v2/lab-journal/{entryAppId}/history` ‚Äî ordered revision list with content snapshots | No history panel / diff viewer in `LabJournalExistingEntry.vue` | `aidocs/37` |
| ~~**PM1a‚ÄìPM1e** Plugin admin~~ | ~~Full `GET/PATCH /v2/admin/plugins` REST surface + CLI~~| **Promoted to ‚úì** ‚Äî `PluginsAdminPane.vue` shipped | `aidocs/16 PM1b` |
| ~~**P10 SQL admin config**~~ | ~~`GET/PATCH /v2/admin/config/sql-timeseries` ‚Äî runtime row + duration caps (V2CONV-A4: moved from `/v2/admin/sql-timeseries/config`)~~ | **Promoted to ‚úì** ‚Äî `AdminSqlTimeseriesPane.vue` + `useSqlTimeseriesConfig` composable + 8 Vitest tests shipped; read-only stats card + Edit dialog (maxRows / maxDuration); RFC 7396 null-to-clear supported; inline ISO-8601 duration + positive-integer validation; replaces `PlaceholderFragmentPane` in `/admin#sql-timeseries`; path collapsed onto generic `/v2/admin/config/{feature}` (V2CONV-A4, 2026-06-03) | `aidocs/29` |

## Standing rule

Per `CLAUDE.md`, this matrix updates in the same PR as any feature
landing or design-doc landing ‚Äî keep it consistent with `aidocs/16`
backlog and `aidocs/00-index.md`. A row that's stale is the bug.

When a UI ships for a dev-track item: remove the row from the Dev Track table above,
promote the row in the relevant section to **‚úì**, and mark the matrix Snapshot date.

---

## 1. DB connectivity / health / migrations

| Capability | Upstream 5.2.0 | This fork | Status | Refs |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Bounded `MigrationsRunner.waitForConnection` w/ exponential backoff | infinite-wait loop | configurable `shepard.migrations.connection-wait-timeout` (default `PT60S`) | **‚úì ‚Üë** | A1 / `aidocs/16` row A1 / `aidocs/17` |
| Per-DB health-check separation (startup vs runtime) | combined / coarse | per-DB `state` + `kind` in `/healthz` | **‚úì ‚Üë** | A1b |
| Graceful degradation when optional DBs (PostGIS) unavailable | endpoints hang | RFC-7807 503 + `Retry-After` when `@RequiresDatabase` not satisfied; 404 when toggle OFF | **‚úì ‚Üë** | A1c |
| `MigrationsRunner.apply()` fail-fast on `MigrationsException` | swallow + log | propagates as `RuntimeException` aborting startup | **‚úì ‚Üë** | A1e (commit `0f2f512`) |
| Automated DB recovery scheduler | none | `@Scheduled(every = "${shepard.health.recovery.interval}")` default `PT15S`; new `quarkus-scheduler` dep | **‚úì ‚Üë** | A1f |
| Parallel DB connectivity checks (startup + recovery) | sequential per-DB | `DbConnectivityWarmer` (startup) + `DbRecoveryScheduler` (recovery tick) both use Java 21 virtual threads; total wait = `max(latencies)` not `sum(latencies)` | **‚úì ‚Üë** | P1 |
| Flyway startup retry ceiling (Mongo/JDBC audit) | unbounded default (Flyway `connect-retries-interval=120s`) | `quarkus.flyway.connect-retries=10` + `connect-retries-interval=PT5S`; ‚âà50s ceiling aligned with Neo4j gate | **‚úì ‚Üë** | A1d (commit `e1c3635`) / `aidocs/17` |
| Migration progress monitoring endpoint | none | `GET /migrations/progress` (P3) | **‚úì ‚Üë** | P3 (commit `7cc74b8`) |
| Readiness check verifies Neo4j migration-chain integrity | none ‚Äî readiness ping only checks connectivity | `neo4j-migration-chain-readiness` SmallRye check (`/shepard/api/healthz/ready`) asserts every classpath `V**` is APPLIED with a matching checksum on the live DB; delegates to `Migrations.validate()` + `Migrations.info(COMPARE)` (same code paths that gate `apply()`); cached per `shepard.health.readiness.max-staleness`; operator runbook `docs/admin/runbooks/migration-chain-integrity.md` with worked example for the UI-020 V61 splice | **‚úì ‚Üë** | OPS-MIGRATION-HEALTHCHECK (2026-05-24) / `aidocs/agent-findings/ops-migration-healthcheck-2026-05-24.md` |

## 2. Configuration / feature toggles

| Capability | Upstream | This fork | Status | Refs |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Build-time vs runtime feature toggle mechanism | `@IfBuildProperty` only | `@ConditionalOnFeature` + runtime-toggleable | **‚úì ‚Üë** | A3 |
| Runtime feature-toggle admin API (`GET /v2/admin/features`, `PATCH /v2/admin/features/{name}`) | none | `FeatureToggleRegistry` + `AdminFeaturesRest`; `@RolesAllowed("instance-admin")`; in-process override, not persisted across restart | **‚úì ‚Üë** | A3b |
| Toggle `source` field (`"default"` / `"config"` / `"runtime"`) on each toggle entry returned by `GET /v2/admin/features` and `PATCH /v2/admin/features/{name}` | none | `FeatureToggleEntry.getSource()` ‚Äî returns `"runtime"` when overridden by PATCH, `"config"` when an `application.properties` key is present, `"default"` otherwise. `FeatureToggleIO` carries the field; no new endpoints, no schema change. 3 new `AdminFeaturesRestTest` cases. | **‚úì ‚Üë** | DX7 |
| Spatial-data namespace alias (`shepard.spatial-data.*` ‚Üí `shepard.infrastructure.spatial.*`) | only old names | both names resolve; old logs deprecation warning; removal v6.0 | **‚úì ‚Üë** | A3c / `aidocs/platform/A3c-namespace-migration.md` |
| Permission cache TTL/max-size config | hard-coded global defaults | `shepard.permissions.cache.ttl` (`PT5M`) + `.max-size` (`10000`) | **‚úì ‚Üë** | A4 |

## 3. Auth / API keys / security

| Capability | Upstream | This fork | Status | Refs |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Semi-permanent API keys with expiry (`validUntil` + JWT `exp`) | none | shipped, distinguishable 401 on expiry | **‚úì ‚Üë** | L5 (commit `30c687a`) |
| `Bearer ` prefix mangle on JWTs containing the literal substring | mangles | safe `startsWith ‚Üí substring(7)` | **‚úì ‚Üë** | M4 |
| Auth-header echo to warn-level logs (token-leak) | full echo | `present`/`absent` only | **‚úì ‚Üë** | M5 |

Returns copy-paste-ready Markdown DMP block pre-filled with `license`, `accessRights`, `embargoEndDate` (latest across DataObjects), `createdByOrcid` (unique ORCIDs across DataObjects), payload kinds, DataObject count. No new entities, no migrations. 8 Mockito unit tests. **UI** (DMP-DOWNLOAD-NAV-01, 2026-05-30): "Download DMP" button on the Collection landing page next to `CiteThisCard.vue` calls the endpoint with `Accept: text/markdown`, downloads via `URL.createObjectURL` + `<a download>`, suggests a `<sanitised-name>-dmp-snippet.md` filename. 9 Vitest cases on the URL builder + filename sanitiser. | **RDM-001 ‚Äî "Cite this dataset" card on Collection landing** (FAIR R1 ‚Äî rich provenance for re-use) | no citation affordance on Collection landing ‚Äî researcher hand-assembles citation from scattered fields | New frontend-only card directly below the Description on the Collection landing page. Renders APA-flavoured plain text / BibTeX / RIS / CSL JSON from existing wire fields (`name`, `createdBy`, `createdAt`, `license` post-LIC1, canonical URL). License-absent path omits the license line entirely. Pure formatter `frontend/utils/citation.ts` + Vuetify `v-tabs` card `frontend/components/context/collection/CiteThisCard.vue` + 46 Vitest cases + Playwright e2e on `/collections/42` and `/collections/661923`. No backend change. Highest per-day-of-effort win from the RDM Scrutinizer pass. Puts Shepard on par with Zenodo / Coscine / Dataverse for the funder-reviewing-the-dataset persona. | **‚úì ‚Üë** (RDM-001) | `aidocs/34` RDM-001, `aidocs/agent-findings/rdm-scrutinizer-2026-05-24.md ¬ßTop-5 #1`, `aidocs/agent-findings/rdm-001-cite-this-dataset-2026-05-24.md` |
| **RDM-005 ‚Äî Metadata Completeness Score widget on Collection landing** (FAIR R1.1 / R1.3 ‚Äî DMP-grade green/amber/red gauge) | no per-Collection FAIR-completeness signal ‚Äî operators had no UI pressure to fill license / accessRights / annotation / ORCID gaps | New frontend-only card between the Cite-this card and the Semantic Annotations section. Renders a red/amber/green score chip (0‚Äì100, red < 50, amber 50‚Äì79, green ‚â• 80) over a 9-check ladder: name + description-‚â•-50-chars + license (LIC1) + accessRights (LIC1) + creator-ORCID (RDM-002) + ‚â•1 semantic annotation + ‚â•1 lab-journal entry + heroImage + ‚â•1 DataObject. Each check carries a "Why this matters" tooltip mapping to DataCite ¬ßN + FAIR sub-principle; missing checks expose a tonal action button that `scrollIntoView`s the relevant on-page edit affordance (description / license-chip-strip / annotations heading / lab-journal panel / hero-image area / DataObjects panel) with a 1.6s primary-glow pulse ‚Äî the ORCID check `router.push("/me")` instead. Pure scorer `frontend/utils/metadataCompleteness.ts` (no I/O, 36 Vitest cases including invariants + per-check pass/fail + band classification + boundary tests). Widget `frontend/components/context/collection/MetadataCompletenessCard.vue` fetches `SemanticAnnotation.getAllCollectionAnnotations` + `useFetchCollectionLabJournalEntries` + `UserApi.getUser` for the three off-shape inputs; auth-settle race fixed via watch on `useAuth().data.accessToken`. 5 Playwright e2e on live (`/collections/42` + `/collections/661923`). No backend change. Live LUMEN + MFFD-Dropbox both score 40/100 (red) at deploy ‚Äî name + description + dataObjects pass, the six R1 fields fail. | **SHACL-1b ‚Äî HMAC audit chain on `:Activity`** ‚Äî per-instance `instance_secret` carried on a `:InstanceConfig` Neo4j singleton (A3b/N1c2/UH1a pattern), seeded on first start from `SHEPARD_INSTANCE_SECRET` env or `SecureRandom`; every `Activity` write is stamped with `HMAC-SHA256(secret_v_n, prevHmac ‚Äñ activityCanonical)` carrying `secretVersion` so rotation never invalidates the chain. Verifier (`HmacChainService.verify`) walks `prev ‚Üí prev.prev ‚Üí ‚Ä¶` and picks the right key per chain segment by `secretVersion`. | **Cross-instance provenance UI** ‚Äî design landed: typed `GET /v2/data-objects/{appId}/provenance` aggregator endpoint over `source_*` attrs + dest createdBy/At + `:Activity` log; new frontend components (`<SourceProvDisplay>`, `<SourceInstanceBadge>`, `<SourceAuthorChip>`, `<SourcePermissionsAudit>`, `<ProvenanceEmptyState>`) rendering a "who authored this on which instance" header strip on DataObject + Collection pages plus an EN 9100 audit pane (‚â§ 3-click test) and a permissions snapshot diff. Closes the today-broken FAIR-R hole where dest shows `createdBy = importer-api-key` for every migrated artefact. M4I-b migration seam ‚Äî the aggregator's substrate switches transparently from opaque attrs to typed PROV-O edges. Backfill UX (`original` vs `backfilled` stamping) surfaces `:Activity`-traceable reconstruction. | **PROV-USER-MIRROR-ENDPOINT ‚Äî `POST /v2/admin/users/mirror` (`:MirroredUser` shadow node, #229)** ‚Äî new `MirroredUser extends AbstractEntity` Neo4j entity; idempotent admin endpoint MERGE on `(sourceInstance, sourceUsername)` pair; 201 on first create, 200 on re-call (same `appId`); V74 migration adds `appId` uniqueness + composite idx; PROV1a auto-captures the POST as an `:Activity`. Fields: `sourceInstance`, `sourceUsername`, `sourceDisplayName?`, `sourceEmail?`, `derivedFrom?` (recursive self-pointer for future multi-hop chains). | **IMP1 ‚Äî dry-run import validation (plan-seal pattern)** ‚Äî `POST /v2/import/validate` dry-runs a manifest (DataObjects + Containers + References) and issues a commitId (plan seal) if structurally valid; `GET /v2/import/plans/{commitId}` retrieves a persisted plan; `GET /v2/import/context` returns a collection state snapshot (DataObject count + fingerprint + optional semantic annotation vocab) so agents can generate consistent manifests. Plans expire 24 h; the `POST /v2/import/jobs` commit endpoint is deferred. In-tree: the commitId / plan-seal contract is core infrastructure on which `shepard-plugin-importer` will build. Backend only (no UI yet). 38 unit tests (35 original + 3 for IMP1 TODO closure). **IMP1 TODO closure:** `GET /v2/import/context?includeSemanticGraph=true` now returns live collection-scoped annotations via `SemanticAnnotationDAO.findByCollectionAppId(String)` ‚Äî previously returned empty list. | none | **IMP1 shipped + IMP1 TODO closed** ‚Äî `ImportPlan` entity + `ImportPlanDAO` + `ImportValidationService` + `ImportV2Rest` + `ImportContextIO`/`ImportManifestIO`/`ImportPlanIO` + `V55` NOOP migration; 38 tests. `SemanticAnnotationDAO.findByCollectionAppId` added. | **‚öô** (IMP1 backend, UI deferred) | `aidocs/34` IMP1 |
| **IMP2 ‚Äî import execute leg (`POST /v2/import/jobs`)** ‚Äî consumes a `commitId` plan seal and runs the manifest. Pre-flight: plan not found ‚Üí 404; USED ‚Üí 409; EXPIRED / null-manifestJson ‚Üí 410; INVALIDATED ‚Üí 422; fingerprint mismatch ‚Üí 409; lock conflict ‚Üí 409. Execution: two-pass DataObject creation (Pass 1 creates without links; Pass 2 wires parent + predecessorIds; successorIds left null to avoid strict-equality guard), then container creation (FILE/TIMESERIES/STRUCTURED_DATA). Plan marked USED even on PARTIAL_FAILURE (commitId is one-shot). Returns 201 `ImportJobResultIO {jobAppId, planCommitId, status, dataObjects, containers, errors}` or 207 on PARTIAL_FAILURE. **IMP2 limitation:** reference wiring (Container‚ÜíDataObject attachment) is NOT performed ‚Äî `ManifestReferenceIO` carries only localRefs, no payload OIDs. Warning added to `errors`. Deferred to IMP3. New classes: `ImportJobsV2Rest`, `ImportExecutionService`, `ImportJobRequestIO`, `ImportJobResultIO`. `ImportPlan` gains `manifestJson` field (stored by `ImportValidationService` from IMP2 onwards). `V83__ImportPlan_manifestJson.cypher` adds `commitId` index. 12 unit tests. Backend only (UI deferred). | none | **IMP2 shipped** ‚Äî `ImportJobsV2Rest` + `ImportExecutionService` + `ImportJobRequestIO` + `ImportJobResultIO` + `ImportPlan.manifestJson` field + `V83` commitId index migration; 12 tests. Reference wiring deferred to IMP3. | **‚öô** (IMP2 backend, UI deferred) | `aidocs/34` IMP2 |
| **IMP-LOCK ‚Äî persistent import-in-progress lock with heartbeat** ‚Äî `:ImportLock` Neo4j entity that survives backend restarts; client importers acquire/heartbeat/release via REST. Six endpoints: `GET /v2/import/lock`, `POST /v2/import/lock` (acquire), `POST /v2/import/lock/{lockId}/heartbeat`, `POST /v2/import/lock/{lockId}/release` (‚Üí COMPLETED), `POST /v2/import/lock/{lockId}/abandon` (‚Üí FAILED), `DELETE /v2/import/lock/{lockId}` (admin cancel). Stale-heartbeat eviction after 5 min (auto-ABANDONED, new lock created). All terminal states preserved in Neo4j for audit. 17 unit tests. Frontend visibility deferred. | none | **IMP-LOCK shipped** ‚Äî `ImportLock` entity + `ImportLockDAO` + `ImportLockService` + `ImportLockV2Rest` + `ImportLockIO` + `V65` constraints migration; 17 tests (now 20 with IMP-DIAG emission verification). | **‚öô** (IMP-LOCK backend, UI deferred) | `aidocs/34` IMP-LOCK |
| **IMP-DIAG ‚Äî structured import diagnostic ring buffer + REST query (#193)** ‚Äî in-memory ring buffer (last 10,000 events per run, 24h TTL) backed by `ConcurrentHashMap<String, Deque<ImportDiagnosticEvent>>`. `runId` = `ImportLock.lockId`. Four new `/v2/` endpoints: `GET /v2/import/diagnostics/{runId}` (event list with optional `?level=` and `?phase=` filters), `GET /v2/import/runs` (run summaries sorted by start time desc), `POST /v2/import/diagnostics/{runId}/events` (ingest single event from Python importer), `POST /v2/import/diagnostics/{runId}/events/batch` (batch ingest). Java-side lifecycle wiring in `ImportLockService`: acquire ‚Üí WARMUP/INFO, release ‚Üí COMPLETE/INFO, abandon ‚Üí COMPLETE/ERROR. External importers push DO_CREATE/REF_ATTACH/FILE_UPLOAD events via the POST ingress. 35 unit tests: 18 (`ImportDiagnosticsLogTest`) + 17 updated (`ImportLockServiceTest`). Frontend deferred. | none | **IMP-DIAG shipped** ‚Äî `ImportDiagnosticEvent` record + `ImportDiagnosticsLog` service + `ImportDiagnosticsIO` shapes + `ImportDiagnosticsV2Rest`; 35 tests. | **‚öô** (IMP-DIAG backend, UI deferred) | `aidocs/34` IMP-DIAG |
| Snapshots (point-in-time, immutable, reproducible reads) | `Version` is a marker only | V2a shipped: `revision: long` counter on every `VersionableEntity` (backfilled by V36; surfaced read-only on all entity IOs). V2b shipped: `Snapshot` + `SnapshotEntry` model; `POST/GET /v2/collections/{appId}/snapshots`; `GET/manifest/DELETE /v2/snapshots/{appId}`; `V40` uniqueness constraint; 29 unit tests (22 + 7); `docs/reference/snapshots.md`. | **Big-bang file-storage migration** (FS1e1) ‚Äî `POST /v2/admin/files/migrate` triggers an async sweep: for each `:ShepardFile` with `providerId = source`, streams bytes from the source adapter to the target adapter (OID preserved via `StoragePutRequest.assignedObjectKey` ‚Äî only `providerId` changes in Neo4j), then deletes from source. `GET /v2/admin/files/migrate/status` polls in-memory state (IDLE / RUNNING / DONE / FAILED). `shepard-admin files migrate <source> <target>` + `shepard-admin files migrate-status` CLI verbs. `GET /v2/admin/storage` returns all discovered adapters with enabled/active state. Frontend: `AdminFileMigrationPane.vue` (506 lines ‚Äî storage-adapter pickers, confirm dialog, live progress bar, per-file rollback dialog) + `useFileMigration.ts` composable (268 lines); mounted at `/admin#file-migration`. Confirmed fully shipped fire-69. Test obligation: `useFileMigration.ts` Vitest tests queued (`PLACEHOLDER-FS1e1-TESTS`). | none | **BE + UI ‚úì** | **‚úì ‚Üë** (FS1e1 ‚Äî BE + UI fully shipped, fire-69) | `aidocs/45 ¬ß6` + `aidocs/34 FS1e1` + `aidocs/16` PLACEHOLDER-REPLACE-FS1e1 + `frontend/components/context/admin/AdminFileMigrationPane.vue` |
| **Per-file rollback fields + endpoint** (FS1e3) ‚Äî four nullable wire-hidden fields on `:ShepardFile` (`previousProviderId`, `previousLocator`, `migratedAt`, `migrationHmac`) capture pre-migration state in the same Cypher SET as the `providerId` swap (left-to-right SET preserves the "stamp before swap" invariant inside one transaction). New `POST /v2/admin/files/migrate/rollback/{appId}` (instance-admin) reads bytes from the current adapter, writes back to the previous adapter using the preserved oid as `assignedObjectKey`, then clears the four bookkeeping fields and restores `providerId`. Refusal: 404 on unknown appId, 409 on "nothing to roll back" (previousProviderId null). Today's fused-Phase-4 `source.delete()` stays per task-spec ("no behaviour split yet ‚Äî just record-keeping"). 13 new unit tests (entity wire-shape regression + Cypher contract + service round-trip + REST exception mapping). V59 NOOP additive cypher migration. This list is **maintained alongside the design docs that propose
each endpoint**; if you add a new design doc that introduces
`/v2/` paths, add a row here in the same PR.

### 14a.4 Convention reminder

- `/v2/<kind>-references/{appId}/...` per-payload-kind read/write
- `/v2/<kind>-containers/{appId}/...` per-container CRUD
- `/v2/admin/...` admin-role gated
- `/users/me` and `/users/{appId}` for profile (no `/v2` prefix ‚Äî
  matches `aidocs/36 ¬ß6`'s decision to put profile at the top
  level for stability)
- `/v2/artifacts/{type}/{id}/url` for any non-payload-kind blob

Plugins (per `aidocs/47 ¬ß2.1`) get their own `/v2/<kind-name>-...`
namespace; core enforces the shape.

| **TemplateKind extension: `PROCESS_RECIPE` + `VIEW_RECIPE`** ‚Äî TPL2 surface; `PROCESS_RECIPE` for manufacturing/process-chain blueprints; `VIEW_RECIPE` for shape-driven projections consumed by `POST /v2/shapes/render`. First concrete `VIEW_RECIPE` consumer: Trace3D (X/Y/Z + scalar ‚Üí color-mapped 3D path). **TPL2a shipped**: allow-list extension in `TemplateBodyValidator` + meta-shape at `backend/src/main/resources/shapes/view-recipe-meta.shacl.ttl` (defines `shepard-ui:ViewRecipe`, `shepard-ui:ChannelBinding` with role + selector + qudt:unit + required). **TPL2b shipped**: `POST /v2/shapes/render` ‚Äî stateless VIEW_RECIPE projection endpoint; takes `{templateAppId, focusShepardId}`; returns `{renderer, channelBindings[{role, channelSelector, unit, required, status="DECLARED", resolved=null}]}`; 422 for non-VIEW_RECIPE kinds; `shapes-render` placeholder registered in frontend placeholderRegistry. | **VIS-S1 ‚Äî `ViewRecipeRenderer` SPI dispatcher** ‚Äî cross-cutting in-tree platform piece for the VIS-* plugin family (vis-trace3d, vis-cad, vis-fem, vis-volume). New SPI under `de.dlr.shepard.spi.view`: `ViewRecipeRenderer` interface + POJO IO records (`RenderRequest` / `RenderResponse` / `RenderException`) + `ViewRecipeRendererRegistry` (`@ApplicationScoped`, ServiceLoader-loaded at startup). The existing `POST /v2/shapes/render` endpoint now reads the requested VIEW_RECIPE template body's `viewRecipeShape` IRI and dispatches to the renderer that claims that shape IRI; absent a claim, falls back to the in-tree TPL2b `DECLARED`-status projection ‚Äî preserving the wire shape for clients whose plugin isn't installed. Pattern mirrors the `PayloadKind` P-series SPI (ServiceLoader, plain-POJO impls). Fail-fast at startup on duplicate shape IRI across two renderers (build-time packaging defect, refuses to start with a clear `IllegalStateException` naming both registrants). Renderer-thrown `RenderException(code, msg)` ‚Üí HTTP 422 with RFC 7807 body; unexpected `RuntimeException` ‚Üí HTTP 500. Three-audience docs: in-tree `docs/reference/view-recipe-spi.md` + `docs/help/plugin-renderer-not-loaded.md`. **Unblocks VIS-T1 sprint-2** (the TraceFrameResolver implementing `ViewRecipeRenderer` for `trace3d:Trace3DViewShape`) + the VIS-C1 / VIS-F1 / VIS-V1 plugin shipment lane. 32 unit tests (14 registry + 18 dispatcher). | n/a | **‚úì shipped (VIS-S1)** ‚Äî VIS-T1 sprint-2 / VIS-C1 / VIS-F1 / VIS-V1 queued (plugin impls in follow-ups) | `aidocs/34` VIS-S1 row ¬∑ `aidocs/16` VIS-S1 row ¬∑ `aidocs/semantics/98 ¬ß1.2` ¬∑ `aidocs/agent-findings/trace3d-spike.md ¬ß3` |
| **V2CONV-B3 ‚Äî `MAPPING_RECIPE` kind + `TransformExecutor` SPI + materialization path** ‚Äî the transform-direction sibling of VIS-S1, and the generic enabler that later dissolves the scene-graph + KRL namespaces (V2CONV-B4/B5). New `templateKind` value `MAPPING_RECIPE` (a recipe binds existing input reference appIds ‚Üí a derived output). New SPI under `de.dlr.shepard.spi.transform`: `TransformExecutor` interface + POJO records (`TransformRequest` / `TransformResult` (REFERENCE\|VIEW) / `TransformException`) + `TransformExecutorRegistry` (`@ApplicationScoped`, ServiceLoader at startup, fail-soft `resolve(iri)` ‚Üí `Optional`, fail-fast on duplicate IRI) ‚Äî mirrors the `ViewRecipeRenderer` SPI exactly. New endpoint `POST /v2/mappings/{templateAppId}/materialize` (dedicated `/v2/mappings` resource ‚Äî distinct "materialize" verb from "render", same shape-IRI ‚Üí executor dispatch): 404 template/executor absent, 422 non-MAPPING_RECIPE / no `mappingRecipeShape`, executor `TransformException` codes ‚Üí 404/422, unexpected ‚Üí 500. Built-in `NoOpTransformExecutor` identity default (claims `‚Ä¶/transform#IdentityTransformShape`, echoes first input reference appId) so the path works with zero plugins. Provenance: typed `EXECUTE` `:Activity` fire-and-forget + skip-capture handoff. Frontend stub `pages/tools/materialize-mapping.vue` + `composables/useMaterializeMapping.ts`. **Scene-graph (B4) + KRL (B5) executors NOT built here** ‚Äî this is the machinery only. 32 JUnit + 6 Vitest. | n/a | **‚úì shipped (V2CONV-B3)** ‚Äî B4/B5 consumers queued | `aidocs/34` V2CONV-B3 row ¬∑ `aidocs/16` V2CONV-B3 row ¬∑ `aidocs/platform/191 ¬ß4` |
| **TPL3a-lite ‚Äî upper-ontology alignment registry** ‚Äî 12 `(:OntologyAlignment)` nodes seeded by V70 migration mapping Shepard concepts to upper-ontology classes (BFO 2020, IAO, PROV-O, IOF Core). | **TPL4 ‚Äî attributes ‚Üí annotations dual-write** ‚Äî backward-compat migration bridge between the legacy `attributes` freetext map on DataObject and the SHACL/ontology annotation layer. Ships two things: (a) `AttributeAnnotationDualWriteService` wired into `DataObjectService.create/update` ‚Äî synthetic `:SemanticAnnotation` nodes with `propertyIRI="urn:shepard:attribute:<key>"`, `valueName=<value>`, `source="attributes-backfill"` ‚Äî gated on deploy-time toggle `shepard.tpl4.dual-write.enabled=false`; (b) `V69` Cypher one-shot backfill for pre-existing DataObjects + rollback `V69_R__...cypher`. Ships: `OntologyGitSource` Neo4j entity + `OntologyGitSourceDAO` + `OntologyGitIngestService` (`ProcessBuilder`-based shallow clone, URL + branch security validation, glob path-pattern file matching, bundle-id namespacing `git-<slug>-<stem>`, delete-and-re-upload for idempotent re-ingest, temp dir cleanup). | **Native JVM MCP server** ‚Äî `quarkus-mcp-server-http:1.9.1` running in the backend JVM at `/v2/mcp/sse`; Phase 1 8-tool surface (`list_collections` / `list_data_objects` / `get_data_object` / `list_channels` / `get_channel_data` with LTTB / `list_files` / `list_structured_data` / `list_annotations`); no HTTP hop / no token relay (tool methods call the service layer directly); auth via `JwtTokenAuthService` (shared with `JWTFilter`) + `McpAuthFilter` (Vert.x `@Observes Filters`, priority 100) + `McpContextBridge` (per-invocation CDI scope principal copy); `DataObjectDAO.findByShepardIdAtDepth` for the get_data_object container detail; user-facing endpoint discovery at `/me#mcp`; coexists with Python sidecar on a different path (`/v2/mcp/sse` vs `/mcp/sse`). **API1 fix (2026-05-26):** `get_data_object` response now includes `timeseriesReferenceAppIds` / `fileReferenceAppIds` / `structuredDataReferenceAppIds` typed arrays (UUID v7 per reference node kind) alongside the existing `containers.timeseries[].containerAppId` path; `get_data_object` tool description updated with explicit warning that containerAppId ‚âÝ referenceAppId. Eliminates the MCP-agent 404 class caused by passing reference-node IDs to `list_channels`. **MCP-COV-03/04/05/11 expansion (2026-05-30):** seven new tools ‚Äî `ts_describe` + `ts_query_multi` (TS-OPT2 bulk wrapper, no 5-tuple in agent contract), `file_upload` + `file_content` (singleton FR1b round-trip, 10 MiB base64 cap), `semantic_annotate_bulk` (N-rows-per-roundtrip sequential), `get_predecessor_chain` + `get_successor_chain` (transitive lineage walk wrapping existing DAO + REST endpoints). 39 new unit tests. **MCP-COV-06/10/12 expansion (2026-05-31):** fourteen further tools across four new catalogues ‚Äî `LabJournalMcpTools.labJournal{List,Create,Update,Delete}` (per-DataObject lab journal CRUD over `LabJournalEntryService`, entity-faithful single `content` field), `VersionMcpTools.version{List,Get}` (Collection-scoped versions over the OGM `uid`), `WatchMcpTools.watch{List,Add,Remove}` (CW1 user-level Collection watching via `CollectionWatcherService`), `ShapesMcpTools.shape{Render,Validate}` + `repExport` (in-tree DECLARED projection + Jena SHACL validate + synchronous TPL14 REP build), `AiMcpTools.ai{Capabilities,Invoke}` (LlmProvider/AiRegistry SPI with the local-noop fail-soft default per the CLAUDE.md "ship a working local default" rule ‚Äî no API key required). 57 new unit tests. **SEARCH-MCP-PERMS-1 + MCP-PERMS-AUDIT-2 (2026-05-31):** `SearchMcpTools.search` now gates every row through its parent-Collection Read walk + per-Collection cache (filter sits between dedupe and pagination, `total` is post-filter); `VersionMcpTools.versionList/versionGet` gate Read on parent Collection via the `:has_version` walk; `ShapesMcpTools.repExport` MCP surface tightens to Write on the Collection because REP records a Collection-scoped PROV-O Activity (REST flip queued under MCP-PERMS-AUDIT-2). 16 new JUnit tests across the three tool catalogues. | none | **‚úì shipped Phase 1 (MCP-2) + API1 fix (2026-05-26) + MCP-COV-03/04/05/06/08/10/11/12/13 expansion (2026-05-30 ‚Üí 2026-05-31)** ‚Äî ~32-tool surface (estimated ~60% of v2 REST coverage); ~185 backend + 4 frontend unit tests; remaining MCP-COV sub-rows (-02 core CRUD, -06 snapshots, -07 SPARQL, -09 KRL) queued. | **‚úì ‚Üë** (MCP-2 + API1 + MCP-COV expansion) | `aidocs/platform/88-quarkus-mcp-server-migration.md` + `aidocs/34` MCP-2 + `aidocs/16` API1 + MCP-COV-03/04/05/06/08/10/11/12/13 |

## Headline state of progress

**Shipped on this fork (vs upstream 5.2.0):** 6 DB-resilience improvements, 5 config/cache improvements, 1 API-key auth feature (L5), 4 security fixes (M2/M4/M5 + the L2a additive identifier substrate), 5 endpoint-additive features (P3, P14, R2/b/c/d/d2), the GitHub Pages docs site with three deploy guides, the **25-channel LUMEN showcase seed + notebook** (15 runs, 2 hold days, 4 signal profiles), **demo auto-seeder** service with bootstrap flow, **Playwright e2e test suite**, API Docs nav link, and **two Live tracking docs** (`aidocs/34` admin-facing + this matrix contributor-facing).

**In flight (agents dispatched):** none currently ‚Äî C5/C5b/L2b/L2c have all landed; the remaining L2 chain (L2d/L2e) is gated on P4 + H4.

**Designed and queued (substantial):** the entire L2 chain after L2a (b/c/d/e), unified search + pagination (`aidocs/13`), semantic-annotation expansion (`aidocs/14`), HDF5/HSDS (A5), Templates (T1), Process design+runtime (PR1), Git integration (G1), User profile (U1), Lab journal v2 + Jupyter (J1), Snapshots (V2), AI features w/ snap-dashboards killer feature (AI1), Admin CLI L1 Phase 2+ (Phase 1 already shipped ‚Äî see ¬ß13 row above), permission-system evolutions (F1-F8), provenance (`aidocs/30`).

**Headline next-horizon line items** (per `aidocs/42` vision):
1. Snap dashboards (AI1e) ‚Äî the killer feature
2. HDF5 / HSDS (A5)
3. Templates + processes (T1 + PR1)
4. User profile + ORCID (U1)

| **TPL-INHERIT ‚Äî `:ShepardTemplate` single-parent inheritance (`parentTemplateAppId: String?`)** ‚Äî an admin template can extend a parent template; the child inherits the parent's flattened definition (JSON-DSL body, reference-creation hints, `iconKey`, semantic-annotation defaults) with the child's own fields overriding on collision. Single-parent for v1 (matches Java/XSD/most schema systems; multi-parent's diamond problem has no demonstrated authoring need). `TemplateInheritanceResolver` walks the chain root-first and deep-merges (objects recurse; arrays merge positionally so `dataobjects[0].attributes` inherits + per-key overrides; `shapeGraph` Turtle concatenated parent-ahead-of-child = `sh:and`). `GET /v2/templates/{appId}?flatten=true` returns the flattened view. `POST`/`PATCH` guard parent existence, kind-match, and cycles (`wouldCreateCycle`); COW carries the parent edge through. | **HMC KIP ‚Äî Vue "Publish" button** (frontend surface for KIP1a; `PublishButton.vue` + `PublishModal.vue` under `frontend/components/context/publish/` mounted on the Collection + DataObject detail panes; SPDX licence picker `CC-BY-4.0 / CC-BY-SA-4.0 / CC0-1.0 / MIT / Apache-2.0 / LGPL-3.0 / GPL-3.0`; post-publish snackbar with copy-to-clipboard for both the PID and the resolver URL) | n/a | **KIP1e shipped** ‚Äî pure frontend slice; calls existing KIP1a endpoints via a new `usePublishEntity` composable (raw `fetch` until the OpenAPI Generator regeneration for KIP1a lands the `PublishApi` client). | **Feature B ‚Äî hero image URL on Collections** | n/a | **‚úì shipped** ‚Äî optional `heroImageUrl` (nullable String) on `Collection` entity. `CollectionIO` read DTO exposes the field; `CollectionService` persists it on create and update. `PATCH /v2/collections/{appId}` (RFC 7396 merge-patch: `null` clears, absent leaves unchanged). No `/shepard/api/` surface touched ‚Äî zero upstream impact. Frontend: `<v-img>` hero banner (220px, cover) above the Collection title on the detail page; hidden when `heroImageUrl` is null. | **ST1a ‚Äî lifecycle `status` field on `DataObject` and `Collection`** | n/a | **shipped** ‚Äî nullable free-form `String status` on `AbstractDataObject` entity (`Collection` + `DataObject` both extend it). `AbstractDataObjectIO` serialises with `@JsonInclude(NON_NULL)`: field is omitted from JSON when null so upstream API clients see no wire change. Suggested values DRAFT / IN_REVIEW / READY / PUBLISHED / ARCHIVED; any free-form string accepted (no server-side state machine). `CollectionService` + `DataObjectService` propagate the field on create + update. Backend-client `Collection.ts`, `DataObject.ts`, `AbstractDataObject.ts` all declare `status?: string | null`. Frontend: `StatusChip.vue` coloured chip shown next to entity name in `TitleAndMetadataDisplay.vue`; clearable `v-select` in both `EditCollectionDescriptionDialog.vue` and `EditDataObjectDescriptionDialog.vue`. No migration needed ‚Äî Neo4j adds the property lazily on next write. | **‚úì ‚Üë** (ST1a) | `aidocs/34` ST1a |
| **IMP1 ‚Äî `shepard-plugin-importer` (agentic data-management pipeline)** | n/a | **üöß IMP1a + IMP1b landed (PRs 1-2 of 7)** ‚Äî plugin module `plugins/importer/` produces `shepard-plugin-importer-${revision}.jar`. **IMP1a (PR-1)**: `ImporterPluginManifest` + `PluginManifest` SPI hook + 4 manifest tests + docs trio. Wired into `backend/pom.xml`'s default-active `with-plugins` profile + self-excluded from every sibling plugin pom (`aas`, `file-s3`, `git`, `hdf5`, `kip`, `minter-{datacite,epic,local}`, `spatial`, `unhide`, `video`) to keep the build-time circular reference acyclic. **IMP1b (PR-2)**: `importer_run` Postgres table via plugin-supplied Flyway migration `V1.11.0` ‚Äî the first concrete instance of `aidocs/platform/32`'s broader JobService design (column set deliberately mirrors that ¬ß3 kernel so a future generic `Job` entity can adopt this table by renaming the backing class without touching SQL or wire shape). Three new classes in `de.dlr.shepard.plugins.importer.runs`: `ImporterRun` (JPA `@Entity`), `ImporterRunRepository` (Panache repo), `ImporterRunService` (mirrors `JobService` interface method-for-method per aidocs/32 ¬ß4). UUID v7 ids minted at submit time. Status enum `PENDING/RUNNING/SUCCEEDED/FAILED/CANCELLED` with `isTerminal()` invariant. Four compound indexes (principal+status, partial-running-progress, partial-terminal-finished, partial-target-collection). Permission boundary at service level (cross-principal row existence not leaked). 28 new unit tests (3 status + 2 entity + 23 service); total 32 tests for the plugin module now. **PR-3..PR-7 queued**: PR-3 extracts `DLRv5Source` from `examples/mffd-showcase/scripts/mffd-dropbox-import.py` v12's `ShepardClient` lines 239-1170; PR-4 the REST surface (`/v2/imports/...`) + scheduler + reaper; PR-5 the `shepard-admin importer ‚Ä¶` CLI; PR-6 the frontend with 2s polling; PR-7 the end-to-end testcontainer integration test.
